### Info
# Nobles
country_event = {
	id = Prov_UI.001
	title = Prov_UI.001.t
	desc = Prov_UI.001.d
	picture = { trigger = { technology_group = western } picture = WE_GN_eventPicture }
	picture = { trigger = { OR = { technology_group = muslim technology_group = ottoman technology_group = steppestech } } picture = ISL_GN_eventPicture }
	picture = { trigger = { OR = { technology_group = eastern technology_group = byzantine } } picture = EE_GN_eventPicture }
	picture = { trigger = { technology_group = indian } picture = IND_GN_eventPicture }
	picture = { trigger = { OR = { technology_group = chinese technology_group = japanese technology_group = southeast_asian technology_group = tibetan } } picture = EA_GN_eventPicture }
	picture = { trigger = { OR = { technology_group = soudantech technology_group = sub_saharan technology_group = central_african technology_group = malagasy_tech technology_group = east_african } } picture = AFR_GN_eventPicture }
	picture = { trigger = { OR = { technology_group = austranesian technology_group = hawaii_tech } } picture = SEA_GN_eventPicture }
	picture = { trigger = { OR = { technology_group = mesoamerican technology_group = south_american } } picture = AMR_GN_eventPicture }

	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = POP_Census.994 } }
	}

	option = {
		name = Prov_UI.001.power
		
		custom_tooltip = NOPowerSources_tooltip

		ai_chance = {
			factor = 0
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = Prov_UI.001.loyalty
		
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 0
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = Prov_UI.001.wealth
		
		custom_tooltip = NO_NatIncome
		custom_tooltip = NO_NatSpend
		
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 0
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = Prov_UI.001.relations

		custom_tooltip = NORelations_tooltip

		ai_chance = {
			factor = 0
		}
	}


	option = {
		name = Prov_UI.001.ruralprp
		custom_tooltip = Prov_UI.001.farmland
		custom_tooltip = Prov_UI.001.mines
		custom_tooltip = Prov_UI.001.forestry
		custom_tooltip = Prov_UI.001.fisheries
		
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 0
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = Prov_UI.001.urbanprp
		custom_tooltip = Prov_UI.001.industrial
		custom_tooltip = Prov_UI.001.academic
		custom_tooltip = Prov_UI.001.commercial
		
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 0
		}
	}


	option = {
		name = PTM_EXIT
		highlight = yes
		
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 100
		}
	}

	after = {
		Unrest_Update = yes
	}
}

### Privileges
# Nobles
country_event = {
	id = Prov_UI.010
	title = no_localisation
	desc = no_localisation
	picture = MEIOU_AND_TAXES_eventPicture

	is_triggered_only = yes
	hidden = yes

	}

		name = PTM_EXIT
		highlight = yes
		country_event = { id = Prov_UI.011 }
	}
}


country_event = {
	id = Prov_UI.011
	title = Prov_NOPrivilegesGrant
	desc = Prov_NOPrivilegesGrant_desc
	picture = { trigger = { technology_group = western } picture = WE_GN_eventPicture }
	picture = { trigger = { OR = { technology_group = muslim technology_group = ottoman technology_group = steppestech } } picture = ISL_GN_eventPicture }
	picture = { trigger = { OR = { technology_group = eastern technology_group = byzantine } } picture = EE_GN_eventPicture }
	picture = { trigger = { technology_group = indian } picture = IND_GN_eventPicture }
	picture = { trigger = { OR = { technology_group = chinese technology_group = japanese technology_group = southeast_asian technology_group = tibetan } } picture = EA_GN_eventPicture }
	picture = { trigger = { OR = { technology_group = soudantech technology_group = sub_saharan technology_group = central_african technology_group = malagasy_tech technology_group = east_african } } picture = AFR_GN_eventPicture }
	picture = { trigger = { OR = { technology_group = austranesian technology_group = hawaii_tech } } picture = SEA_GN_eventPicture }
	picture = { trigger = { OR = { technology_group = mesoamerican technology_group = south_american } } picture = AMR_GN_eventPicture }

	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 1
	}
	
	trigger = {
		check_key = { lhs = Prov_NOPow value = 1 }
	}
	
	immediate = {
	}

	option = {
		name = PTM_EXIT
		trigger = {
			ai = yes
		}
		highlight = yes
		
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 4.5
		}
	}
	# Noble Dues
	option = {
		name = Privilege_NOTaxERaise_title
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				AND = {
					ai = no
					NOT = { Privilege_Has = { Privilege=NOTaxE Lvl=5 } }
				}
				AND = {
					Privilege_Has = { Privilege=NOTaxE Lvl=0 }
					Privilege_NOTaxE1CanRaise = yes
				}
				AND = {
					Privilege_Has = { Privilege=NOTaxE Lvl=1 }
					Privilege_NOTaxE2CanRaise = yes
				}
				AND = {
					Privilege_Has = { Privilege=NOTaxE Lvl=2 }
					Privilege_NOTaxE3CanRaise = yes
				}
				AND = {
					Privilege_Has = { Privilege=NOTaxE Lvl=3 }
					Privilege_NOTaxE4CanRaise = yes
				}
				AND = {
					Privilege_Has = { Privilege=NOTaxE Lvl=4 }
					Privilege_NOTaxE5CanRaise = yes
				}
			}
		}
		set_country_flag = ProvUI_Action
		Privilege_NOTaxERaise = yes
		log ="SYS-Politics:[GetYear]:[This.GetName]:granted Noble Dues Privilege to:Nobles:+:[This.GovernmentName]"
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 0 #stopped for AI, as restoring the previous level costs way more from what is gained when such exemption is granted
		}
	}
	# Noble Service
	option = {
		name = Privilege_NOServiceERaise_title
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				AND = {
					ai = no
					NOT = { Privilege_Has = { Privilege=NOServiceE Lvl=5 } }
				}
				AND = {
					Privilege_Has = { Privilege=NOServiceE Lvl=0 }
					Privilege_NOServiceE1CanRaise = yes
				}
				AND = {
					Privilege_Has = { Privilege=NOServiceE Lvl=1 }
					Privilege_NOServiceE2CanRaise = yes
				}
				AND = {
					Privilege_Has = { Privilege=NOServiceE Lvl=2 }
					Privilege_NOServiceE3CanRaise = yes
				}
				AND = {
					Privilege_Has = { Privilege=NOServiceE Lvl=3 }
					Privilege_NOServiceE4CanRaise = yes
				}
				AND = {
					Privilege_Has = { Privilege=NOServiceE Lvl=4 }
					Privilege_NOServiceE5CanRaise = yes
				}
			}
		}
		log ="SYS-Politics:[GetYear]:[This.GetName]:increased Noble Service Privilege to:Nobles"
		set_country_flag = ProvUI_Action
		Privilege_NOServiceERaise = { costs = yes }
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 0 #stopped for AI, as restoring the previous level costs way more from what is gained when such exemption is granted
		}
	}
	# Processing Monopoly
	option = {
		name = Privilege_NOProcessingRaise_title
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				AND = {
					ai = no
					NOT = { Privilege_Has = { Privilege=NOProcessing Lvl=2 } }
				}
				AND = {
					Privilege_Has = { Privilege=NOProcessing Lvl=0 }
					Privilege_NOProcessing1CanRaise = yes
				}
				AND = {
					Privilege_Has = { Privilege=NOProcessing Lvl=1 }
					Privilege_NOProcessing2CanRaise = yes
				}
			}
		}
		set_country_flag = ProvUI_Action
		Privilege_NOProcessingRaise = yes
		log ="SYS-Politics:[GetYear]:[This.GetName]:increased Processing Monopoly Privilege to:Nobles"
		
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 0 #stopped for AI, as restoring the previous level costs way more from what is gained when such exemption is granted

			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				OR = {
					NOT = {has_country_flag = 	AI_Interaction_IncLoyNO_HighInterest}
					has_country_flag = 	AI_Interaction_DecPowNO_HighInterest
					has_country_flag = 	AI_Interaction_DecPowNO_MedInterest
				}
			}
		}
	}
	# Game Monopoly
	option = {
		name = Privilege_NOGameRaise_title
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				AND = {
					ai = no

					Privilege_NOAutonomy4CanRaise = yes
				}
				AND = {
					Privilege_Has = { Privilege=NOAutonomy Lvl=4 }
					Privilege_NOAutonomy5CanRaise = yes
				}
			}
		}
		set_country_flag = ProvUI_Action
		Privilege_NOAutonomyRaise = yes
		log ="SYS-Politics:[GetYear]:[This.GetName]:increased Rural Autonomy Privilege to:Nobles"
		
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 0 #stopped for AI, as restoring the previous level costs way more from what is gained when such exemption is granted

			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				OR = {
					NOT = {has_country_flag = 	AI_Interaction_IncLoyNO_HighInterest}
					has_country_flag = 	AI_Interaction_DecPowNO_HighInterest
					has_country_flag = 	AI_Interaction_DecPowNO_MedInterest
				}
			}
		}
	}
	# Prestigious Diplomacy
	option = {
		name = Privilege_NODiplomacyRaise_title
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				AND = {
					ai = no
					NOT = { Privilege_Has = { Privilege=NODiplomacy Lvl=2 } }

country_event = {
	id = Prov_UI.019
	title = Prov_BUPrivilegesGrant
	desc = Prov_BUPrivilegesGrant_desc
	picture = ECONOMY_eventPicture

	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 1
	}
	
	trigger = {
		OR = {
			ai = no
			check_key = { lhs = Prov_BUPow value = 1 }
		}
	}
	
	immediate = {

	}
	option = {
		name = PTM_EXIT
		trigger = {
			ai = yes
		}
		highlight = yes
		
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 4.5
		}
	}
	# Sale of Office
	option = {
		name = Privilege_BUOfficeRaise_title
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				AND = {
					ai = no
					NOT = { Privilege_Has = { Privilege=BUOffice Lvl=2 } }
				}
				AND = {
					Privilege_Has = { Privilege=BUOffice Lvl=0 }
					Privilege_BUOffice1CanRaise = yes
				}
				AND = {
					Privilege_Has = { Privilege=BUOffice Lvl=1 }
					Privilege_BUOffice2CanRaise = yes
				}
			}
		}
		set_country_flag = ProvUI_Action
		Privilege_BUOfficeRaise = yes
		if = {
			limit = {
				ai = yes
				OR = {
					AND = {
						NOT = {Privilege_Has = { Privilege=BUOffice Lvl=0 }}
						NOT = { faction_influence = { faction = FC_BU influence = 30 } }
					}
					NOT = { faction_influence = { faction = FC_BU influence = 20 } }
				}
			}
			#boost BU faction
			BU_FactionBoost = yes
			log = "SYS-Politics:[GetYear]:[This.GetName]:Boost Faction:Bureaucrats:+:[This.GovernmentName]:::for priv"
			add_adm_power = -10
			add_dip_power = -10
			Pol_FacInfReactPosMajor = { Fac=BU }
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { check_key = { lhs = Prov_BUPow value = 20 } }
				}
				Stab_Subtract25Percent = yes
			}
			set_key = { lhs = Prov_React value = 3 }
			set_key = { lhs = Prov_ReactSrc value = 5 }
			#country_event = { id = Prov_React.001 }
		}
		log ="SYS-Politics:[GetYear]:[This.GetName]:revoked Sale of Office Privilege (more formal) to:Bureaucrats:+:[This.GovernmentName]"
		
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 20

			modifier = { 
				factor = 0
				NOT = {
					has_country_flag = AI_Reform_BUOffice
					has_country_flag = AI_Interaction_DecCrptLaws_HighInterest
					has_country_flag = AI_Interaction_DecCrptLaws_MedInterest
					has_country_flag = AI_Interaction_DecCrptLaws_LowInterest
				}
			}

			modifier = { 
				factor = 1.5
				has_country_flag = AI_Interaction_DecCrptLaws_HighInterest
			}

			modifier = { 
				factor = 0.75
				NOT = {
					has_country_flag = AI_Reform_BUOffice
					has_country_flag = AI_Interaction_DecCrptLaws_HighInterest
				}
			}
			
			modifier = { 
				factor = 0.2
				NOT = {
					has_country_flag = AI_Reform_BUOffice
					has_country_flag = AI_Interaction_DecCrptLaws_HighInterest
					has_country_flag = AI_Interaction_DecCrptLaws_MedInterest
				}
			}

			modifier = { 
				factor = 0.1
				AI_Interaction_stability_MedInterest = yes #interaction causes -1 stability hit
			}

			modifier = { 
				factor = 0
				OR = {
					AI_Interaction_stability_HighInterest = yes #interaction causes -1 stability hit
					Rights_AIReadyToReform = yes
					check_key = { lhs = Prov_BULoy value = 65 } #AI should bring it down with anti-corruption measures first
					corruption = 60 #AI should bring it down with anti-corruption measures first
					NOT = { check_key = { lhs = Prov_NOLoy value = 40 } } #only small hit to loyalty
					NOT = { check_key = { lhs = NO_RelationState value = -30 } }
				}
			}
		}
	}

				OR = {
					Rights_AIReadyToReform = yes
					check_key = { lhs = Prov_BULoy value = 70 } #AI should bring it down with anti-corruption measures first, it gives a temporary increase
					corruption = 50					
				}			
			}
		}
	}
	# Institutional Oversight
	option = {
		name = Privilege_BUOversightRaise_title
		trigger = {
			Privilege_HasGreater = { Privilege=BUHierarchy Lvl=1 }
			OR = {
				AND = {
					ai = no
					NOT = { Privilege_Has = { Privilege=BUOversight Lvl=2 } }
				}
				AND = {
					Privilege_Has = { Privilege=BUOversight Lvl=0 }
					Privilege_BUOversight1CanRaise = yes
				}
				AND = {
					Privilege_Has = { Privilege=BUOversight Lvl=1 }
					Privilege_BUOversight2CanRaise = yes
				}
			}
		}
		set_country_flag = ProvUI_Action
		Privilege_BUOversightRaise = { event=Prov_UI.018 }
		if = {
			limit = {
				ai = yes
				OR = {
					AND = {
						Privilege_Has = { Privilege=BUOversight Lvl=0 }
						NOT = { faction_influence = { faction = FC_BU influence = 30 } }
					}
					AND = {
						Privilege_Has = { Privilege=BUOversight Lvl=1 }
						NOT = { faction_influence = { faction = FC_BU influence = 40 } }
					}
				}
			}
			#boost BU faction
			BU_FactionBoost = yes
			log = "SYS-Politics:[GetYear]:[This.GetName]:Boost Faction:Bureaucrats:+:[This.GovernmentName]:::for priv"
			add_adm_power = -10
			add_dip_power = -10
			Pol_FacInfReactPosMajor = { Fac=BU }
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { check_key = { lhs = Prov_BUPow value = 20 } }
				}
				Stab_Subtract25Percent = yes
			}
			set_key = { lhs = Prov_React value = 3 }
			set_key = { lhs = Prov_ReactSrc value = 5 }
			#country_event = { id = Prov_React.001 }
		}
		log ="SYS-Politics:[GetYear]:[This.GetName]:revoked Institutional Oversight Privilege (more formal) to:Bureaucrats:+:[This.GovernmentName]"

		ai_chance = {
			factor = 10

			modifier = { 
				factor = 0
				NOT = {
					has_country_flag = AI_Reform_BUOversight
					has_country_flag = AI_Interaction_DecCrptLaws_HighInterest
					has_country_flag = AI_Interaction_DecCrptLaws_MedInterest
					current_income_balance = 0
				}
			}
			modifier = { 
				factor = 1.1
				has_country_flag = AI_Interaction_DecCrptLaws_HighInterest
			}
			modifier = { 
				factor = 0.1
				NOT = {
					has_country_flag = AI_Reform_BUOversight
					has_country_flag = AI_Interaction_DecCrptLaws_HighInterest
					AND = {
						has_country_flag = AI_Interaction_DecCrptLaws_MedInterest
						current_income_balance = 0
					}
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.5
				AI_Interaction_stability_MedInterest = yes #interaction causes -1 stability hit
			}

			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				OR = {
					AI_Interaction_stability_HighInterest = yes #interaction causes -1 stability hit
					Rights_AIReadyToReform = yes
					check_key = { lhs = Prov_BULoy value = 70 } #AI should bring it down with anti-corruption measures first, it gives a temporary increase
					corruption = 50
					NOT = { check_key = { lhs = Prov_NOLoy value = 55 } } 
					NOT = { check_key = { lhs = NO_RelationState value = -30 } } 
				}
			}
		}
	}

						Privilege_Has = { Privilege=BUEnlist Lvl=0 }
						NOT = { check_key = { lhs = Prov_NOPow value = 70 } }
						check_key = { lhs = Prov_BUPow value = 40 }
					}
					AND = { #first level of the privilege is useful if state reach is getting too high, as it may stop other reforms
						Privilege_Has = { Privilege=BUEnlist Lvl=0 }
						check_key = { lhs = Prov_BUPow value = 55 }
					}
					AND = { #second level of the privilege is useful if NO Power is already below 60%, as country is already quite reformed and increase to tax efficiency is worth increase to elite power
						Privilege_Has = { Privilege=BUEnlist Lvl=1 }
						NOT = { check_key = { lhs = Prov_NOPow value = 60 } }

	id = Prov_UI.021
	title = Prov_NOPrivilegesRevoke
	desc = Prov_NOPrivilegesRevoke_desc
	picture = { trigger = { technology_group = western } picture = WE_GN_eventPicture }
	picture = { trigger = { OR = { technology_group = muslim technology_group = ottoman technology_group = steppestech } } picture = ISL_GN_eventPicture }
	picture = { trigger = { OR = { technology_group = eastern technology_group = byzantine } } picture = EE_GN_eventPicture }
	picture = { trigger = { technology_group = indian } picture = IND_GN_eventPicture }
	picture = { trigger = { OR = { technology_group = chinese technology_group = japanese technology_group = southeast_asian technology_group = tibetan } } picture = EA_GN_eventPicture }
	picture = { trigger = { OR = { technology_group = soudantech technology_group = sub_saharan technology_group = central_african technology_group = malagasy_tech technology_group = east_african } } picture = AFR_GN_eventPicture }
	picture = { trigger = { OR = { technology_group = austranesian technology_group = hawaii_tech } } picture = SEA_GN_eventPicture }
	picture = { trigger = { OR = { technology_group = mesoamerican technology_group = south_american } } picture = AMR_GN_eventPicture }

	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 1
	}
	
	trigger = {

	}
	
	immediate = {

	}
	option = {
		name = PTM_EXIT
		highlight = yes
		trigger = {
			ai = yes
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 3
			modifier = { #temporary, will be moved to each option
				factor = 100
				Rights_AIReadyToReform = yes 
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 5
				is_at_war = yes
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 3
				is_at_war = yes
				NOT = { Rights_NOSer2HasGreater = yes }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 2
				is_at_war = yes
				NOT = { Rights_NOSer3HasGreater = yes }
			}
		}
	}
	# Noble Dues
	option = {
		name = Privilege_NOTaxELower_title
		trigger = {
   			Privilege_HasGreater = { Privilege=NOTaxE Lvl=1 }
			OR = {
				AND = {
					ai = no
					Privilege_HasGreater = { Privilege=NOTaxE Lvl=1 }
				}
				AND = {
					Privilege_Has = { Privilege=NOTaxE Lvl=1 }
					Privilege_NOTaxE0CanLower = yes
				}
				AND = {
					Privilege_Has = { Privilege=NOTaxE Lvl=2 }
					Privilege_NOTaxE1CanLower = yes
				}
				AND = {
					Privilege_Has = { Privilege=NOTaxE Lvl=3 }
					Privilege_NOTaxE2CanLower = yes
				}
				AND = {
					Privilege_Has = { Privilege=NOTaxE Lvl=4 }
					Privilege_NOTaxE3CanLower = yes
				}
				AND = {
					Privilege_Has = { Privilege=NOTaxE Lvl=5 }
					Privilege_NOTaxE4CanLower = yes
				}
			}
		}
		set_country_flag = ProvUI_Action
		Privilege_NOTaxELower = yes
		log ="SYS-Politics:[GetYear]:[This.GetName]:reduced Noble Dues Privilege to:Nobles"

		ai_chance = {
			factor = 5 #high factor as loyalty check comes from AI_Interaction_IncLoyNo flag

			modifier = { 
				factor = 0
				NOT = {
					OR = {
						has_country_flag = AI_Reform_NOTaxE
						AND = {
							has_country_flag = AI_Interaction_DecPowNO_HighInterest
							Privilege_HasGreater = { Privilege=NOTaxE Lvl=2 } #if obligations are low (3) or lower, target them to decrease NO power
						}
					}
				}
			}

			modifier = { 
				factor = 0
				OR = {
					has_country_flag = AI_Interaction_IncLoyNO_HighInterest
					AI_Interaction_stability_HighInterest = yes
				}
			}
			modifier = { 
				factor = 0.4
				OR = {
					has_country_flag = AI_Interaction_IncLoyNO_MedInterest
					AI_Interaction_stability_MedInterest = yes
				}
			}	
			modifier = { 
				factor = 0.6
				OR = {
					has_country_flag = AI_Interaction_IncLoyNO_LowInterest
					AI_Interaction_stability_LowInterest = yes
				}
			}
			modifier = { 
				factor = 0.4
				Privilege_Has = { Privilege=NOTaxE Lvl=2 } #if obligations are already moderate (2), something else should be targetted
			}
			modifier = { 
				factor = 0.1
				Privilege_Has = { Privilege=NOTaxE Lvl=1 } #if obligations are already high (1), something else should be targetted
			}	
		}
	}

	# Processing Monopoly
	option = {
		name = Privilege_NOProcessingLower_title
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				AND = {
					ai = no
					Privilege_HasGreater = { Privilege=NOProcessing Lvl=1 }
				}
				AND = {
					Privilege_Has = { Privilege=NOProcessing Lvl=1 }
					Privilege_NOProcessing0CanLower = yes
				}
				AND = {
					Privilege_Has = { Privilege=NOProcessing Lvl=2 }
					Privilege_NOProcessing1CanLower = yes
				}
			}
		}
		set_country_flag = ProvUI_Action
		Privilege_NOProcessingLower = yes
		log ="SYS-Politics:[GetYear]:[This.GetName]:reduced Processing Monopoly Privilege to:Nobles"

		ai_chance = {
			factor = 10 

			modifier = { 
				factor = 0.1 #low factor, as this privilege is not essential to strip down and costs AI too much NO loyalty in the early game
				NOT = { has_country_flag = AI_Reform_NOProcessing }
			}

			modifier = { 
				factor = 0 #only scenario to remove monopoly is to have AI Reform goal and to already have quite high NO loyalty
				NOT = {
					OR = {
						has_country_flag = AI_Reform_NOProcessing
						AND = {
							has_country_flag = AI_Interaction_DecPowNO_HighInterest
							Privilege_Has = { Privilege=NOProcessing Lvl=2 } #if monopoly is full, target it to decrease NO power
						}
					}
				}
			}

			modifier = { 
				factor = 0
				OR = {
					has_country_flag = AI_Interaction_IncLoyNO_HighInterest
					AI_Interaction_stability_HighInterest = yes
				}
			}
			modifier = { 
				factor = 0.5
				OR = {
					has_country_flag = AI_Interaction_IncLoyNO_MedInterest
					AI_Interaction_stability_MedInterest = yes
				}
			}	
			modifier = { 
				factor = 0.75
				OR = {
					has_country_flag = AI_Interaction_IncLoyNO_LowInterest
					AI_Interaction_stability_LowInterest = yes
				}
			}			
		}

				}

					Privilege_Has = { Privilege=NOHierarchy Lvl=1 }
					Privilege_NOHierarchy0CanLower = yes
				}
				AND = {
					Privilege_Has = { Privilege=NOHierarchy Lvl=2 }
					Privilege_NOHierarchy1CanLower = yes
				}
				AND = {
					Privilege_Has = { Privilege=NOHierarchy Lvl=3 }
					Privilege_NOHierarchy2CanLower = yes
				}
			}
		}
		set_country_flag = ProvUI_Action
		Privilege_NOHierarchyLower = yes
		log ="SYS-Politics:[GetYear]:[This.GetName]:reduced Noble Hierarchy Privilege to:Nobles"

		ai_chance = {
			factor = 10 #high factor as loyalty check comes from AI_Interaction_IncLoyNo flag

			modifier = { 
				factor = 0
				NOT = {
					has_country_flag = AI_Reform_NOHierarchy
					AND = {
						has_country_flag = AI_Reform_NOGov
						Rights_NOGov4HasGreater = yes
						check_key = { lhs = Prov_NOPow value = 55 }
					}
					AND = {
						has_country_flag = AI_Reform_NOSer
						Rights_NOSer5HasGreater = yes
						check_key = { lhs = Prov_NOPow value = 55 }
					}
				}
			}

			modifier = { 
				factor = 0.5
				NOT = {
					check_key = { lhs = Prov_BUPow value = 25 } ## too soon
				}
			}

			modifier = { 
				factor = 0
				NOT = {
					check_key = { lhs = Prov_BUPow value = 15 } ## too soon
				}
			}

			modifier = { 
				factor = 0
				OR = {
					has_country_flag = AI_Interaction_IncLoyNO_HighInterest
					AI_Interaction_stability_HighInterest = yes
				}
			}
			modifier = { 
				factor = 0.2
				OR = {
					has_country_flag = AI_Interaction_IncLoyNO_MedInterest
					AI_Interaction_stability_MedInterest = yes
				}
			}	
			modifier = { 
				factor = 0.4
				OR = {
					has_country_flag = AI_Interaction_IncLoyNO_LowInterest
					AI_Interaction_stability_LowInterest = yes
				}
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = PTM_EXIT
		highlight = yes
		trigger = {
			ai = no
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 2
			modifier = { #temporary, will be moved to each option
				factor = 100
				Rights_AIReadyToReform = yes 
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 5
				is_at_war = yes
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 3
				is_at_war = yes
				NOT = { Rights_NOSer2HasGreater = yes }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 2
				is_at_war = yes
				NOT = { Rights_NOSer3HasGreater = yes }
			}
		}
	}

	after = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					ai = no
					has_country_flag = ProvUI_Action
				}
			}
			clr_country_flag = ProvUI_Action
			Nat_Update = yes
			Unrest_Update = yes
			AI_Interactions_Recalc = yes
		}
	}
}

# Noble interactions
country_event = {
	id = Prov_UI.040
	title = Prov_UI.040.t
	desc = Prov_UI.040.d
	picture = { trigger = { technology_group = western } picture = WE_GN_eventPicture }
	picture = { trigger = { OR = { technology_group = muslim technology_group = ottoman technology_group = steppestech } } picture = ISL_GN_eventPicture }
	picture = { trigger = { OR = { technology_group = eastern technology_group = byzantine } } picture = EE_GN_eventPicture }
	picture = { trigger = { technology_group = indian } picture = IND_GN_eventPicture }
	picture = { trigger = { OR = { technology_group = chinese technology_group = japanese technology_group = southeast_asian technology_group = tibetan } } picture = EA_GN_eventPicture }
	picture = { trigger = { OR = { technology_group = soudantech technology_group = sub_saharan technology_group = central_african technology_group = malagasy_tech technology_group = east_african } } picture = AFR_GN_eventPicture }
	picture = { trigger = { OR = { technology_group = austranesian technology_group = hawaii_tech } } picture = SEA_GN_eventPicture }
	picture = { trigger = { OR = { technology_group = mesoamerican technology_group = south_american } } picture = AMR_GN_eventPicture }

	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 1
	}
	
	trigger = {
		check_key = { lhs = Prov_NOPow value = 1 }
	}
	
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			random_owned_province = {
				limit = {
					isValidProv = yes
				}
				save_event_target_as = consort_home
			}
			random_owned_province = {
				limit = {
					isValidProv = yes
					check_key = { lhs = Prov_NOPow which = event_target:consort_home }
				}
				save_event_target_as = consort_home
			}
			random_owned_province = {
				limit = {
					isValidProv = yes
					check_key = { lhs = Prov_NOPow which = event_target:consort_home }
				}
				save_event_target_as = consort_home
			}
			random_owned_province = {
				limit = {
					isValidProv = yes
					check_key = { lhs = Prov_NOPow which = event_target:consort_home }
				}
				save_event_target_as = consort_home
			}
			Pol_AdvisorGenerateCabinet = { Faction = NO Var1=Pol_Tmp0 Var2=Pol_Tmp1 Var3=Pol_Tmp2 }
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = PTM_EXIT
		trigger = {
			ai = yes
		}
		highlight = yes
		
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 1.5
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.666
				NOT = { check_key = { lhs = Prov_NOLoy value = 50 } }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.5
				NOT = { check_key = { lhs = Prov_NOLoy value = 20 } }
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = NO_FactionBoost_t
		trigger = {
			Fac_HasNO = yes
			ai = no
			Fac_CanCrackdownOrBoost = yes
		}

		set_country_flag = ProvUI_Action
		NO_FactionBoost = yes
		log ="SYS-Politics:[GetYear]:[This.GetName]:Boost Faction:Nobles:+:[This.GovernmentName]"
		
		add_dip_power = -10
		add_mil_power = -5
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { check_key = { lhs = Prov_NOPow value = 20 } }
			}
			Stab_Subtract25Percent = yes
		}
		Pol_FacInfReactPosMajor = { Fac=NO }

		custom_tooltip = Rights_LB
		custom_tooltip = Rights_EveryProvince
		if = {
			limit = {
				faction_influence = {
					faction = FC_NO
					influence = 50
				}
			}
			Public_ChangePowerbrokerLoyaltyTooltipProv = { Powerbroker=NO Amount=15 }
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				faction_influence = {
					faction = FC_NO
					influence = 25
				}
			}
			Public_ChangePowerbrokerLoyaltyTooltipProv = { Powerbroker=NO Amount=10 }
		}
		else = {
			Public_ChangePowerbrokerLoyaltyTooltipProv = { Powerbroker=NO Amount=5 }
		}

		custom_tooltip = Rights_LB
		custom_tooltip = POP_NegReact
		hidden_effect = {
			set_key = { lhs = Prov_React value = 3 }
			set_key = { lhs = Prov_ReactSrc value = 1 }
			#country_event = { id = Prov_React.001 }
		}
		
		custom_tooltip = NO_FactionBoost_expl

		hidden_effect = {
			change_key = { lhs = NO_Favors value = 2 }
		}

		
		
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 1
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				check_key = { lhs = Prov_BUPow value = 25 }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.5
				check_key = { lhs = Prov_BUPow value = 20 }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.5
				check_key = { lhs = Prov_BUPow value = 15 }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.5
				check_key = { lhs = Prov_BUPow value = 10 }
			}

			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				# if there is no need to increase loyalty, do not use the interaction
				NOT = { has_country_flag = AI_Interaction_IncLoyNO_HighInterest }
				NOT = { has_country_flag = AI_Interaction_IncLoyNO_MedInterest }
				NOT = { has_country_flag = AI_Interaction_IncLoyNO_LowInterest }
			}
			
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				Rights_AIReadyToReform = yes
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				faction_influence = {
					faction = FC_NO
					influence = 85
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.5
				faction_influence = {
					faction = FC_NO
					influence = 75
				}
			}
		}
	}

	#Provide Land Grants
	option = {
		name = NO_LandGrant_t
		trigger = {
			NOT = { has_country_modifier = Prov_LandGrantCD }
			NOT = { has_country_flag = LandInt_Block }
			ai = no
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { has_country_flag = LandInt_Block }
			}
			hidden_effect = {
			set_key = { lhs = LandInt_Mode value = 0 }
			set_key = { lhs = LandInt_Class value = 0 }
			set_key = { lhs = LandInt_Class2 value = 3 }
			}
			country_event = {
				id = SYS_LandInteraction.001
			}
			custom_tooltip = NO_LandGrant_expl
		}
		else = {
			custom_tooltip = LandInt_Block
		}
		
		
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 0
		}
	}
	
	#Promote Lesser Nobility
	option = {
		name = NO_RecruitLords_t
		trigger = {
			Rights_NOGov6HasGreater = no
			NOT = { has_country_modifier = NO_Promotion_S }
			NOT = { has_country_modifier = NO_Promotion_M }

	#Disown an Unpopular Relative
	option = {

		name = BG_CommerceDrive_t
		trigger = {
			Rights_BGCom4HasGreater = yes
			NOT = { has_country_modifier = BG_CommerceDrive_S }
			NOT = { has_country_modifier = BG_CommerceDrive_M }
			NOT = { has_country_modifier = BG_CommerceDrive_L }

			NOT = { has_country_modifier = BG_RestrictTrade_M }
			NOT = { has_country_modifier = BG_RestrictTrade_L }
		}

		add_dip_power = -10
		Pol_FacInfReactPos = { Fac=BG }

			limit = {
				has_country_flag = medici_system_triggers_active

					has_country_modifier = gonfaloniere_artigiani
				}
				custom_tooltip = medici_system_add_cost_gonfaloniere_artigiani
				add_dip_power = -10
				add_adm_power = -10
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					has_country_modifier = gonfaloniere_mercanti
				}
				custom_tooltip = medici_system_sub_cost_gonfaloniere_mercanti
				add_dip_power = 5
			}

			custom_tooltip = mercanti_little_add
			hidden_effect = {
				change_variable = {
					which = "mercanti_favor"
					value = 1
				}
			}
			
			custom_tooltip = artigiani_little_sub
			hidden_effect = {
				change_variable = {
					which = "artigiani_favor"
					value = -1
				}
			}
			
			recalculate_medici_faction_relation_modifiers = yes
		}

		custom_tooltip = Rights_LB
		custom_tooltip = Rights_EveryProvince
		custom_tooltip = BG_CommerceDrive_effect
		Public_ChangePowerbrokerLoyaltyTooltipProv = { Powerbroker=BG Amount=5 }

		custom_tooltip = BG_CommerceDrive_expl

		hidden_effect = {
			change_key = { lhs = BG_Favors value = 1 }
		}

			factor = 1

			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				# if there is no need to increase loyalty nor power, do not use the interaction
				NOT = {has_country_flag = AI_Interaction_IncLoyBG_HighInterest}
				NOT = {has_country_flag = AI_Interaction_IncLoyBG_MedInterest}
				NOT = {has_country_flag = AI_Interaction_IncLoyBG_LowInterest}
				NOT = {has_country_flag = AI_Interaction_IncPowBG_HighInterest}
				NOT = {has_country_flag = AI_Interaction_IncPowBG_MedInterest}
				NOT = {has_country_flag = AI_Interaction_IncPowBG_LowInterest}
			}
			
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.25
				NOT = {has_country_flag = AI_Interaction_IncLoyBG_HighInterest}
				NOT = {has_country_flag = AI_Interaction_IncLoyBG_MedInterest}
				NOT = {has_country_flag = AI_Interaction_IncPowBG_HighInterest}
				NOT = {has_country_flag = AI_Interaction_IncPowBG_MedInterest}
			}

				factor = 0.2
				num_of_loans = 1
			}

	option = {
		name = PTM_EXIT
		highlight = yes

		trigger = {
			ai = no
		}		
		
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 0.7
		}
	}

	after = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					ai = no
					has_country_flag = ProvUI_Action
				}
			}
			clr_country_flag = ProvUI_Action
			Nat_Update = yes
			Unrest_Update = yes
			AI_Interactions_Recalc = yes
		}
	}

					faction = FC_CL
					influence = 25
				}
			}

		}

		}

		#custom_tooltip = Rights_EveryProvince
		Public_ChangeConcernTooltipProv = { Concern=Spirituality Amount=1 }
		Public_ChangePowerbrokerLoyaltyTooltipProv = { Powerbroker=CL Amount=15 }

		custom_tooltip = CL_ProvideDonationsLavish_expl

		hidden_effect = {
			change_key = { lhs = CL_Favors value = 1 }
		}
		
		if = {
			limit = { religion = catholic }
			add_reform_desire = -0.00001
		}

		ai_chance = {
			factor = 0.3

			modifier = {
				factor = 2
				years_of_income = 5
			}

			modifier = {
				factor = 0.2
				NOT = { years_of_income = 3 }
			}

			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				# if there is no need to increase loyalty nor power, do not use the interaction
				NOT = {has_country_flag = AI_Interaction_IncLoyCL_HighInterest}
				NOT = {has_country_flag = AI_Interaction_IncLoyCL_MedInterest}
				NOT = {has_country_flag = AI_Interaction_IncLoyCL_LowInterest}
				NOT = {has_country_flag = AI_Interaction_IncPowCL_HighInterest}
				NOT = {has_country_flag = AI_Interaction_IncPowCL_MedInterest}
				NOT = {has_country_flag = AI_Interaction_IncPowCL_LowInterest}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				#do not empower if there is any pressure to limit their power
				OR = {
					has_country_flag = AI_Interaction_DecPowCL_HighInterest
					has_country_flag = AI_Interaction_DecPowCL_MedInterest
					has_country_flag = AI_Interaction_DecPowCL_LowInterest
				}				
			}
		}
	}

	#Perform a Show of Devotion
	option = {
		name = CL_Devotion_t
		trigger = {
			NOT = { has_country_modifier = CL_Devotion_S }
			NOT = { has_country_modifier = CL_Devotion_M }
			NOT = { has_country_modifier = CL_Devotion_L }
		}
		log ="SYS-Politics:[GetYear]:[This.GetName]:Perform a Show of Devotion:Clergy:+:[This.GovernmentName]"

		set_country_flag = ProvUI_Action
		CL_Devotion = yes
		add_prestige = -10
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_key = { lhs = Prov_CLPow value = 65 }
			}
			add_adm_power = -30
			add_dip_power = -30
			add_mil_power = -30
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				check_key = { lhs = Prov_CLPow value = 35 }
			}
			add_adm_power = -20
			add_dip_power = -20
			add_mil_power = -20
		}
		else = {
			add_adm_power = -10
			add_dip_power = -10
			add_mil_power = -10
		}
		#custom_tooltip = CL_Devotion_effect
		Pol_FacInfReactPos = { Fac=CL }

		custom_tooltip = Rights_LB
		custom_tooltip = Rights_EveryProvince
		Public_ChangeConcernTooltipProv = { Concern=Spirituality Amount=1 }
		Public_ChangePowerbrokerLoyaltyTooltipProv = { Powerbroker=CL Amount=10 }

		custom_tooltip = CL_Devotion_expl

		hidden_effect = {
			change_key = { lhs = CL_Favors value = 1 }
		}

		ai_chance = {
			factor = 0.25

			modifier = {
				factor = 0.5
				NOT = { prestige = 50 } #if there is no dire need, do not waste prestige
			}

			modifier = {
				factor = 0.25
				NOT = { prestige = 20 } #if there is no dire need, do not waste prestige
			}

			modifier = {
				factor = 2
				has_country_flag = AI_Interaction_IncLoyCL_HighInterest
			}

			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				# if there is no need to increase loyalty, don't use the interaction
				NOT = { has_country_flag = AI_Interaction_IncLoyCL_HighInterest }
				NOT = { has_country_flag = AI_Interaction_IncLoyCL_MedInterest }
			}
		}
	}

		add_legitimacy = -5 # Immediate loss for Clans
		add_horde_unity = -5 # Immediate loss for Clans

		custom_tooltip = TR_SupportRights_effect
		Public_ChangePowerbrokerLoyaltyTooltipProv = { Powerbroker=TR Amount=5 }

		hidden_effect = {
			change_key = { lhs = TR_Favors value = 1 }
		}

		ai_chance = {
			factor = 1
			
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				horde_unity = 80
			}
			#interaction gives horde unity as its most important effect, let AI use it to tackle this
			modifier = {
				factor = 2
				NOT = { horde_unity = 60 }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 2
				NOT = { horde_unity = 50 }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 2
				NOT = { horde_unity = 40 }
			}

			modifier = {
				factor = 0 #avoid loosing legitimacy if it is seeked
				OR = {
					has_country_flag = AI_Interaction_legitimacy_equivalent_HighInterest
					has_country_flag = AI_Interaction_legitimacy_equivalent_MedInterest
				}
			}
			modifier = { #avoid wasting mana if power <5%
				factor = 0
				NOT = {check_key = { lhs = Prov_TRPow value = 5 } }
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = TR_ClanMarriageState_t
		trigger = {
			is_nomad = no
			is_tribal = no
			NOT = { government = theocracy }
			NOT = { has_country_modifier = TR_ClanMarriageClans_S }

				factor = 0
				NOT = { has_country_flag = AI_Interaction_IncLoyTR_HighInterest } #use only if absolutely needed (AI is poor with rebels)
				NOT = { has_country_flag = AI_Interaction_IncLoyTR_MedInterest } #use only if absolutely needed (AI is poor with rebels)
				NOT = { has_country_flag = AI_Interaction_IncLoyTR_LowInterest } #use only if absolutely needed (AI is poor with rebels)
			}

			modifier = {
				factor = 0 #avoid loosing legitimacy if it is seeked
				OR = {
					has_country_flag = AI_Interaction_legitimacy_equivalent_HighInterest
					has_country_flag = AI_Interaction_legitimacy_equivalent_MedInterest
					has_country_flag = AI_Interaction_legitimacy_equivalent_LowInterest

			}
			
			modifier = { #avoid wasting mana if power <5%
				factor = 0
				NOT = {check_key = { lhs = Prov_TRPow value = 5 } }
			}
		}
	}

		}

		}

country_event = {
	id = Prov_UI.060
	title = Prov_UI.060.t
	desc = Prov_UI.060.d
	picture = { trigger = { technology_group = western } picture = WE_GN_eventPicture }
	picture = { trigger = { OR = { technology_group = muslim technology_group = ottoman technology_group = steppestech } } picture = ISL_GN_eventPicture }
	picture = { trigger = { OR = { technology_group = eastern technology_group = byzantine } } picture = EE_GN_eventPicture }
	picture = { trigger = { technology_group = indian } picture = IND_GN_eventPicture }
	picture = { trigger = { OR = { technology_group = chinese technology_group = japanese technology_group = southeast_asian technology_group = tibetan } } picture = EA_GN_eventPicture }
	picture = { trigger = { OR = { technology_group = soudantech technology_group = sub_saharan technology_group = central_african technology_group = malagasy_tech technology_group = east_african } } picture = AFR_GN_eventPicture }
	picture = { trigger = { OR = { technology_group = austranesian technology_group = hawaii_tech } } picture = SEA_GN_eventPicture }
	picture = { trigger = { OR = { technology_group = mesoamerican technology_group = south_american } } picture = AMR_GN_eventPicture }

	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 1
	}
	
	trigger = {
		check_key = { lhs = Prov_NOPow value = 1 }
	}
	
	immediate = {
	}

	option = {
		name = PTM_EXIT
		highlight = yes
		
		trigger = {
			ai = yes
		}

		ai_chance = {
			factor = 1.5
		
			modifier = {
				factor = 2
				NOT = { 
					check_key = { lhs = Prov_NOLoy value = 70 } #do not spend loyalty until collected enough
				}
			}
		
			modifier = {
				factor = 2
				NOT = { 
					check_key = { lhs = Prov_NOLoy value = 50 } #do not spend loyalty until collected enough
				}
			}
		
			modifier = {
				factor = 3
				NOT = { 
					check_key = { lhs = Prov_NOLoy value = 30 } #do not spend loyalty until collected enough
				}
			}
		}
	}

	#Crackdown on Aristocratic Faction
	option = {
		name = NO_FactionCrackdown_t 
		trigger = {
			ai = no
			Fac_HasNO = yes
			faction_influence = {
				faction = FC_NO
				influence = 10
			}
			Fac_CanCrackdownOrBoost = yes
		}
		log ="SYS-Politics:[GetYear]:[This.GetName]:Crackdown on Faction:Nobles:-:[This.GovernmentName]"

		set_country_flag = ProvUI_Action
		NO_FactionCrackdown = yes
		add_dip_power = -5
		add_mil_power = -15
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_key = { lhs = Prov_NOPow value = 65 }
			}
			Stab_Subtract25Percent = yes
		}

		custom_tooltip = Rights_LB
		custom_tooltip = Rights_EveryProvince
		if = {
			limit = {
				faction_influence = {
					faction = FC_NO
					influence = 50
				}
			}
			Public_ChangePowerbrokerLoyaltyTooltipProv = { Powerbroker=NO Amount=-20 }
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				faction_influence = {
					faction = FC_NO
					influence = 25
				}
			}
			Public_ChangePowerbrokerLoyaltyTooltipProv = { Powerbroker=NO Amount=-15 }
		}
		else = {
			Public_ChangePowerbrokerLoyaltyTooltipProv = { Powerbroker=NO Amount=-10 }
		}

		custom_tooltip = Rights_LB
		Pol_ChangeRelationsStateTooltip = { NO=yes type=value val=-30 }
		
		custom_tooltip = NO_FactionCrackdown_expl

		hidden_effect = {
			change_key = { lhs = NO_Favors value = -4 }
		}

		ai_chance = {
			factor = 0 
		}
	}
	
	#Expropriate Land
	option = {
		name = NO_LandExpropriate_t
		trigger = {
			NOT = { has_country_modifier = Prov_LandExpropriateCD }
			NOT = { has_country_flag = LandInt_Block }
			OR = {
				ai = no
				stability = 1 # only expropriate when having stability >= 1
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			set_key = { lhs = LandInt_Mode value = 1 }
			set_key = { lhs = LandInt_Class value = 3 }
			set_key = { lhs = LandInt_Class2 value = 0 }
		}
		country_event = {
			id = SYS_LandInteraction.001
		}
		custom_tooltip = NO_LandExpropriate_expl
		
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 1
			#previously modified by Prov_TRPow (high TRPow -> less interaction)
			#previously modified by Prov_NOLoy (high NOLoy -> more interaction)
			#previously modified by BU_PrpResources (high BU_PrpResources -> less interaction)
			#previously modified by Prov_NOPow (high Prov_NOPow -> more interaction)
			
			modifier = { 
				factor = 1.5
				stability = 2
			}

			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				is_at_war = yes
			}
			
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				OR = {
					has_country_flag = AI_Interaction_IncLoyNO_HighInterest
					has_country_flag = AI_Interaction_IncLoyNO_MedInterest
					Rights_AIReadyToReform = yes
				}
			}
			
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.25
				has_country_flag = AI_Interaction_IncLoyNO_LowInterest				
			}
			
			#group of checks for NO being stripped from privileges supporting their high power
			modifier = {
				factor = 0 #no sense to demote if there is no taxation in place
				OR = {
					Rights_BUTax1Has = yes
					Rights_NOGov1Has = yes
				}
			}
			
			modifier = {
				factor = 0 #no sense to demote if there are all privileges to opress peasantry in place
				OR = {
					AND = {
						Privilege_Has = { Privilege=NOProcessing Lvl=2 }
						Privilege_Has = { Privilege=NOForestry Lvl=2 }
						Privilege_Has = { Privilege=NOGame Lvl=2 }
					}
					Privilege_Has = { Privilege=NOSeigneurial Lvl=2 }
					Privilege_Has = { Privilege=NOSeigneurial Lvl=3 }
				}
			}
			
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.5
				Rights_NOGov5Has = yes
			}

			modifier = {
				factor = 3 #high interest
				has_country_flag = AI_Interaction_DecPowNO_HighInterest
			}

			modifier = {
				factor = 2 #medium interest
				has_country_flag = AI_Interaction_DecPowNO_MedInterest
			}

				factor = 0
				NOT = { 
					OR = {
						has_country_flag = AI_Interaction_DecPowNO_HighInterest
						has_country_flag = AI_Interaction_DecPowNO_MedInterest
						has_country_flag = AI_Interaction_DecPowNO_LowInterest

	#Demote Greater Nobility
	option = {
		name = NO_DemoteLords_t
		trigger = {
			NOT = { has_country_modifier = NO_DemoteLords_S }
			NOT = { has_country_modifier = NO_DemoteLords_M }
			NOT = { has_country_modifier = NO_DemoteLords_L }
			NOT = { has_country_modifier = NO_Promotion_S }
			NOT = { has_country_modifier = NO_Promotion_M }
			NOT = { has_country_modifier = NO_Promotion_L }
			Rights_NOGov6HasGreater = no
		}
		log ="SYS-Politics:[GetYear]:[This.GetName]:Demote Greater Nobility:Nobles:-:[This.GovernmentName]"

		set_country_flag = ProvUI_Action
		NO_DemoteLords = yes
		add_dip_power = -5
		add_mil_power = -15
		Pol_FacInfReact = { Fac=NO }
		Pol_ProvStabSet8 = { Prov=NO }

		custom_tooltip = Rights_LB
		custom_tooltip = Rights_EveryProvince
		custom_tooltip = NO_DemoteLords_effect
		Public_ChangePowerbrokerLoyaltyTooltipProv = { Powerbroker=NO Amount=-25 }

		custom_tooltip = NO_DemoteLords_expl

		hidden_effect = {
			change_key = { lhs = NO_Favors value = -3 }
		}
		
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 1

			modifier = {
				factor = 1.5
				stability = 0 # stability at least 0
				NOT = { has_country_flag = AI_Interaction_IncLoyNO_HighInterest } # If in need of loyalty dont increase likelyhood
				OR = {
					AND = {
						### Able to do NOGov2->3 by privileges but power is too high
						NOT = { Privilege_HasGreater = { Privilege=NOProcessing Lvl=2 } }
						NOT = { Privilege_HasGreater = { Privilege=NOGame Lvl=2 } }
						NOT = { Privilege_HasGreater = { Privilege=NOForestry Lvl=2 } }
						NOT = { Privilege_HasGreater = { Privilege=NOSeigneurial Lvl=3 } }
						check_key = { lhs = Prov_NOPow value = 85 }
					}
					AND = {
						### Able to do NOGov3->4 by privileges but power is too high
						check_key = { lhs = Prov_NOPow value = 70 }
   						NOT = { Privilege_HasGreater = { Privilege=NOSeigneurial Lvl=2 } }
					}
					AND = {
						### Able to do NOSer1->2 by requirements but power is too high
						check_key = { lhs = Prov_NOPow value = 85 }
						mil_idea_group_amount = { amount = 1 }
						Privilege_HasGreater = { Privilege=BUStructure Lvl=1 }
						check_key = { lhs = Prov_BUPow value = 10 }
					}
					AND = {
						### Able to do NOSer2->3 by requirements but power is too high
						check_key = { lhs = Prov_NOPow value = 80 }
						mil_idea_group_amount = { amount = 2 }
						check_key = { lhs = Prov_BUPow value = 20 }
					}
				}
			}

			modifier = { # High interest in decreasing power, low interest in increasing loyalty
				factor = 1.25
				has_country_flag = AI_Interaction_DecPowNO_HighInterest
				stability = 1
				has_country_flag = AI_Interaction_IncLoyNO_LowInterest
			}

			modifier = {
				factor = 0.5
				has_country_flag = AI_Interaction_DecPowNO_MedInterest
			}

			modifier = {
				factor = 0.1
				has_country_flag = AI_Interaction_DecPowNO_LowInterest
			}

			modifier = { 
				factor = 0.5
				NOT = { stability = 1 }
			}

			#do not use interaction if there is no need from AI interaction flags meant to reduce NO Power
			modifier = { 
				factor = 0
				NOT = { 
					has_country_flag = AI_Interaction_DecPowNO_HighInterest
					has_country_flag = AI_Interaction_DecPowNO_MedInterest
					has_country_flag = AI_Interaction_DecPowNO_LowInterest
				}
			}

			modifier = { ## Dont use if stability is below 0
				factor = 0
				NOT = { stability = 0 }
			}
			
			#group of checks for NO being stripped from privileges supporting their high power
			modifier = {
				factor = 0 #no sense to demote if there is no taxation in place
				OR = {
					Rights_BUTax1Has = yes
					AND = { # If Gov1->2 reform cannot be done dont demote
						Rights_NOGov1Has = yes
   						Privilege_HasGreater = { Privilege=NOHierarchy Lvl=3 }
					}
				}
			}
			
			modifier = {
				factor = 0 #no sense to demote if there are all privileges to opress peasantry in place
				OR = {
					AND = {
						Privilege_Has = { Privilege=NOProcessing Lvl=2 }
						Privilege_Has = { Privilege=NOForestry Lvl=2 }
						Privilege_Has = { Privilege=NOGame Lvl=2 }
					}
					Privilege_Has = { Privilege=NOSeigneurial Lvl=2 }
					Privilege_Has = { Privilege=NOSeigneurial Lvl=3 }
				}
			}
			
			#blockade when getting ready to enact a reform
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				OR = {
					AND = {
						OR = {
							has_country_flag = AI_Interaction_IncLoyNO_HighInterest 
							is_at_war = yes
						}
						NOT = { Rights_NOSer3HasGreater = yes } #do not demote if your army relies on nobles (also because power will bounce right back)
					}
					Rights_AIReadyToReform = yes
				}
			}
		}
	}

			NOT = { has_country_modifier = CL_RallyFaithful_M }
			NOT = { has_country_modifier = CL_RallyFaithful_L }
		}
		log ="SYS-Politics:[GetYear]:[This.GetName]:Rally the faithful:Clergy:-:[This.GovernmentName]"

		set_country_flag = ProvUI_Action
		CL_RallyFaithful = yes
		add_mil_power = -20
		Pol_FacInfReact = { Fac=CL }

		custom_tooltip = Rights_LB
		custom_tooltip = Rights_EveryProvince
		#custom_tooltip = CL_RallyFaithful_effect
		Public_ChangePowerbrokerLoyaltyTooltipProv = { Powerbroker=CL Amount=-10 }

		custom_tooltip = CL_RallyFaithful_expl

		hidden_effect = {
			change_key = { lhs = CL_Favors value = -2 }
		}
		
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 0.25

			modifier = { 
				factor = 0
				OR = { 
					has_country_flag = AI_Interaction_IncLoyCL_HighInterest
					has_country_flag = AI_Interaction_IncLoyCL_MedInterest
				}
			}
				
			
			modifier = {
				factor = 2
				NOT = { manpower_percentage	= 0.25 } #low manpower
			}

			modifier = {
				factor = 3
				NOT = { manpower_percentage	= 0.15 } #low manpower
			}

			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				stability = 0 #if both stability and manpower are fine, no need for support
				manpower_percentage	= 0.45 #if both stability and manpower are fine, no need for support
			}

			modifier = {
				factor = 2
				tag = TUR
			}
		}
	}

	#Compel Dynastic Endorsement
	option = {
		name = CL_Dynasty_t
		trigger = {
			NOT = { has_country_modifier = CL_Dynasty_S }
			NOT = { has_country_modifier = CL_Dynasty_M }
			NOT = { has_country_modifier = CL_Dynasty_L }
			government = monarchy
		}
		log ="SYS-Politics:[GetYear]:[This.GetName]:Compel Dynastic Endorsement:Clergy:-:[This.GovernmentName]"

		set_country_flag = ProvUI_Action
		CL_Dynasty = yes
		add_dip_power = -30
		Pol_FacInfReact = { Fac=CL }

		custom_tooltip = Rights_LB
		custom_tooltip = Rights_EveryProvince
		#custom_tooltip = CL_Dynasty_effect
		Public_ChangePowerbrokerLoyaltyTooltipProv = { Powerbroker=CL Amount=-15 }

		custom_tooltip = CL_Dynasty_expl

		hidden_effect = {
			change_key = { lhs = CL_Favors value = -2 }
		}
		
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 2

			modifier = {
				factor = 0 #use only if legitimacy is seeked
				NOT = { has_country_flag = AI_Interaction_legitimacy_equivalent_HighInterest}
				NOT = { has_country_flag = AI_Interaction_legitimacy_equivalent_MedInterest}
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = PTM_EXIT
		highlight = yes
		
		trigger = {
			ai = no
		}

		ai_chance = {
			factor = 1
			modifier = {
				factor = 2
				NOT = { check_key = { lhs = Prov_CLLoy value = 40 } }
			}
		}
	}

	after = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					ai = no
					has_country_flag = ProvUI_Action
				}
			}
			clr_country_flag = ProvUI_Action
			Nat_Update = yes
			Unrest_Update = yes
			AI_Interactions_Recalc = yes
		}
	}

	option = {

			check_key = { lhs = Admin_Hire value = 10 }
		}

			country_event = { id = Prov_UI.084 }
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = Admin_HireLower10
		trigger = {
			check_key = { lhs = Admin_Hire value = 15 }
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			subtract_key = { lhs = Admin_Hire value = 10 }
			country_event = { id = Prov_UI.084 }
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = PTM_BACK
		highlight = yes
		
		country_event = { id = Prov_UI.081 }
	}

	option = {
		name = PTM_EXIT
		highlight = yes
		
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 100
		}

country_event = {
	id = Prov_UI.436
	title = Prov_UI.436.title
	desc = Prov_UI.436.desc
	picture = all_church_state

	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			ReligionSize_Country = yes
			every_owned_province = {
				MN_Missionary = yes
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "Prov_UI.436.optaa" #Religion of the Realm
		trigger = { western_christian = yes }
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_key = { lhs = Prov_CLLoy value = 40 }
				NOT = { check_key = { lhs = Prov_CLPow value = 70 } }
				OR = { is_religion_enabled = waldensian is_religion_enabled = lollard is_religion_enabled = hussite is_religion_enabled = protestant is_religion_enabled = reformed }
			}
			custom_tooltip = Rights_UI_AllOf
			custom_tooltip = POP_CLHasLoy_40
			custom_tooltip = POP_CLNotHasPow_70
			custom_tooltip = DGRealmReligion
			custom_tooltip = realm_religion_tt
			hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = DG_Convert.301 } }
		}
		else = {
			custom_tooltip = Rights_UI_AllOf
			custom_tooltip = POP_CLHasLoy_40
			custom_tooltip = POP_CLNotHasPow_70
			custom_tooltip = DGRealmReligion
			custom_tooltip = realm_religion_tt
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 0
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = "Prov_UI.436.optba" #Organise the Missionaries
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_key = { lhs = Prov_CLLoy value = 40 }
				NOT = { check_key = { lhs = Prov_CLPow value = 70 } }
				any_owned_province = {
					isValidProv = yes
					OR = {
						has_missionary = yes
						AND = {
							has_province_flag = UI_Select
							NOT = { religion = owner }
							check_key = { lhs = MN_S0MStrength value = 0.3 }
						}
						AND = {
							has_province_flag = UI_Select
							religion = owner
							OR = {
								check_key = { lhs = MN_S1MStrength value = 0.3 }
								check_key = { lhs = MN_S2MStrength value = 0.3 }
								check_key = { lhs = MN_S3MStrength value = 0.3 }
								check_key = { lhs = MN_S4MStrength value = 0.3 }
								check_key = { lhs = MN_S5MStrength value = 0.3 }
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
			custom_tooltip = Rights_UI_AllOf
			custom_tooltip = POP_CLHasLoy_40
			custom_tooltip = POP_CLNotHasPow_70
			custom_tooltip = DGMissionary
			custom_tooltip = missionary_organisation_tt
			hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = DG_Convert.101 } }
		}
		else = {
			custom_tooltip = Rights_UI_AllOf
			custom_tooltip = POP_CLHasLoy_40
			custom_tooltip = POP_CLNotHasPow_70
			custom_tooltip = DGMissionary
			custom_tooltip = missionary_organisation_tt
			hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = DG_Convert.101 } }
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 0
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = "Prov_UI.436.optca" #Establlish an Inquisition
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_key = { lhs = Prov_CLLoy value = 40 }
				NOT = { check_key = { lhs = Prov_CLPow value = 70 } }
				NOT = { has_country_modifier = evangel_cm }
			}
			custom_tooltip = Rights_UI_AllOf
			custom_tooltip = POP_CLHasLoy_40
			custom_tooltip = POP_CLNotHasPow_70
			custom_tooltip = DGInquisition
			custom_tooltip = inquisition_organisation_tt
			hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = DG_Inquisition.001 } }
		}
		else = {
			custom_tooltip = Rights_UI_AllOf
			custom_tooltip = POP_CLHasLoy_40
			custom_tooltip = POP_CLNotHasPow_70
			custom_tooltip = DGInquisition
			custom_tooltip = inquisition_organisation_tt
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 0
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = "Prov_UI.436.optda" #Beacon of the [Root.Religion.GetName] Faith
		trigger = { western_christian = yes }
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_key = { lhs = Prov_CLLoy value = 40 }
				NOT = { check_key = { lhs = Prov_CLPow value = 70 } }
			}
			custom_tooltip = Rights_UI_AllOf
			custom_tooltip = POP_CLHasLoy_40
			custom_tooltip = POP_CLNotHasPow_70
			custom_tooltip = DGBeacon
			custom_tooltip = faith_beacon_tt
			hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = DG_Convert.201 } }
		}
		else = {
			custom_tooltip = Rights_UI_AllOf
			custom_tooltip = POP_CLHasLoy_40
			custom_tooltip = POP_CLNotHasPow_70
			custom_tooltip = DGBeacon
			custom_tooltip = faith_beacon_tt
		}
		
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 0
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = PTM_EXIT
		highlight = yes
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 100
		}
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = Prov_UI.437
	title = Prov_UI.437.title
	desc = "Prov_UI.437.desc"
	picture = all_church_state

	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = "Prov_UI.437.optaa" #Indulgences
		trigger = {
			western_christian = yes
			NOT = { is_key_equal = { lhs = aspect_07 value = 3 } }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				is_key_equal = { lhs = aspect_07 value = 1 }
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { check_key = { lhs = Prov_CLPow value = 50 } }
					check_key = { lhs = Prov_BUPow value = 25 }
				}
				custom_tooltip = Rights_UI_AllOf
				custom_tooltip = POP_CLNotHasPow_50
				custom_tooltip = POP_BUHasPow_25
				custom_tooltip = indulgence_condemn_one_tt
				custom_tooltip = tenet_change_cost_tt
				Privilege_ManaCost = { adm_power=50 dip_power=250 }
				Public_ChangePowerbrokerLoyaltyTooltipProv = { Powerbroker=CL Amount=-20 }
				add_corruption = 5
				hidden_effect = { indulgence_condemnation_se = yes }
				if = {
					limit = { religion = catholic }
					if = {
						limit = { PAP = { is_key_equal = { lhs = aspect_07 value = 1 } } }
						PAP = { add_opinion = { who = ROOT modifier = change_tenet_hate } }
					}
					else_if = {
						limit = { PAP = { is_key_equal = { lhs = aspect_07 value = 3 } } }
						PAP = { add_opinion = { who = ROOT modifier = change_tenet_thrilled } }
					}
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = { religion = avignonist }
					if = {
						limit = { AVI = { is_key_equal = { lhs = aspect_07 value = 1 } } }
						AVI = { add_opinion = { who = ROOT modifier = change_tenet_hate } }
					}
					else_if = {
						limit = { AVI = { is_key_equal = { lhs = aspect_07 value = 3 } } }
						AVI = { add_opinion = { who = ROOT modifier = change_tenet_thrilled } }
					}
				}
				if = {
					limit = { any_known_country = { religion = ROOT NOT = { tag = PAP } NOT = { tag = AVI } is_key_equal = { lhs = aspect_07 value = 1 } } }
					custom_tooltip = indulgence_condemn_negative_tt
					hidden_effect = {
						every_known_country = {
							limit = { religion = ROOT NOT = { tag = PAP } NOT = { tag = AVI } is_key_equal = { lhs = aspect_07 value = 1 } }

					}

							limit = { is_key_equal = { lhs = aspect_07 value = 3 } }
							add_opinion = { who = ROOT modifier = change_tenet_like }
						}
					}
				}
			}
			else = {
				custom_tooltip = Rights_UI_AllOf

				custom_tooltip = POP_BUHasPow_25
				custom_tooltip = indulgence_condemn_one_tt
				custom_tooltip = tenet_change_cost_tt
				custom_tooltip = indulgence_cost_one_tt
				custom_tooltip = diplomatic_impact_tt
				if = {
					limit = { religion = catholic }
					if = { limit = { PAP = { is_key_equal = { lhs = aspect_07 value = 1 } } } custom_tooltip = indulgence_pope_negative_tt }
					else_if = { limit = { PAP = { is_key_equal = { lhs = aspect_07 value = 3 } } } custom_tooltip = indulgence_pope_positive_tt }
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = { religion = avignonist }
					if = { limit = { AVI = { is_key_equal = { lhs = aspect_07 value = 1 } } } custom_tooltip = indulgence_pope_negative_tt }
					else_if = { limit = { AVI = { is_key_equal = { lhs = aspect_07 value = 3 } } } custom_tooltip = indulgence_pope_positive_tt }
				}
				custom_tooltip = indulgence_condemn_negative_tt
				custom_tooltip = indulgence_condemn_positive_tt
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				is_key_equal = { lhs = aspect_07 value = 2 }
			}

country_event = {
    id = Prov_UI.what
    title = Prov_UI.What_title
    desc = Prov_UI.512.Nat_Stockpiles
	picture = BIG_BOOK_eventPicture

    is_triggered_only = yes

    immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { check_key = { lhs = Tmp_0 value = 0 } }
				}
				set_key = { lhs = Tmp_0 value = 0 }
			}
			Effect_512_Helper = yes
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = Prov_UI.512_FUND
		custom_tooltip = Prov_UI.5112_FUND_desc
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					check_key = { lhs = Tmp_0 value = 0 }
				}
				Set_Funds_Based_On_Flag = yes
				scaled_ducat_cost_country = { input = Tmp_0 }
			}
		}
		hidden_country_event = { id = Prov_UI.5112_food }
	}
	option = {
		name = Prov_UI.512_food_reset
		hidden_effect = { set_key = { lhs = Tmp_0 value = 0 } }
		hidden_country_event = { id = Prov_UI.5112_food }
	}

	option = {
		name = Prov_UI.512_food_10
		hidden_effect = { change_key = { lhs = Tmp_0 value = 10 } }
		hidden_country_event = { id = Prov_UI.5112_food }
	}
	option = {
		name = Prov_UI.512_food_20
		hidden_effect = { change_key = { lhs = Tmp_0 value = 20 } }
		hidden_country_event = { id = Prov_UI.5112_food }
	}
	option = {
		name = Prov_UI.512_food_50
		hidden_effect = { change_key = { lhs = Tmp_0 value = 50 } }
		hidden_country_event = { id = Prov_UI.5112_food }
	}
	option = {
		name = Prov_UI.512_food_100
		hidden_effect = { change_key = { lhs = Tmp_0 value = 100 } }
		hidden_country_event = { id = Prov_UI.5112_food }
	}	
	option = {
		name = Prov_UI.512_food_10_sub
		hidden_effect = { change_key = { lhs = Tmp_0 value = -10 } }
		hidden_country_event = { id = Prov_UI.5112_food }
	}
	option = {
		name = Prov_UI.512_food_20_sub
		hidden_effect = { change_key = { lhs = Tmp_0 value = -20 } }
		hidden_country_event = { id = Prov_UI.5112_food }
	}
	option = {
		name = Prov_UI.512_food_50_sub
		hidden_effect = { change_key = { lhs = Tmp_0 value = -50 } }
		hidden_country_event = { id = Prov_UI.5112_food }
	}
	option = {
		name = Prov_UI.5112_food_100_sub
		hidden_effect = { change_key = { lhs = Tmp_0 value = -100 } }
		hidden_country_event = { id = Prov_UI.5112_food }
	}
	
	option = {
		name = PTM_BACK
		hidden_country_event = { id = Prov_UI.512 }
	}

		name = PTM_EXIT
	}
